From Robert.Day at metaswitch.com  Wed Aug  5 03:37:51 2015
From: Robert.Day at metaswitch.com (Robert Day)
Date: Wed, 5 Aug 2015 07:37:51 +0000
Subject: [Clearwater] King Lear release note
Message-ID: <CY1PR0201MB092469362AF972E0C42806D2F4750@CY1PR0201MB0924.namprd02.prod.outlook.com>

Hi all,

The release for sprint "King Lear" has been cut.  The code for this release is tagged as release-78 in Github.

The main new feature in this release is the addition of per-function, per-type SIP statistics, meaning you can now query (for example) how many successful incoming INVITE transactions your BGCF has handled recently - see http://clearwater.readthedocs.org/en/latest/Clearwater_SNMP_Statistics/index.html for more details. We've also enhanced Cacti to graph the S-CSCF INVITE statistics - see http://clearwater.readthedocs.org/en/latest/Cacti/index.html for instructions and our Cacti templates.

This release includes the following bug fixes:


*         401 responses from S-CSCF to I-CSCF only SAS logged on the receiving side.  (https://github.com/Metaswitch/sprout/issues/1142)

*         OPTIONS polls are logged to SAS but can't be searched for (https://github.com/Metaswitch/sprout/issues/677)

*         DNS queries leak a DnsTsx each time (https://github.com/Metaswitch/cpp-common/issues/350)

*         IPv6 DNS servers aren't supported (https://github.com/Metaswitch/cpp-common/issues/246)

*         "knife cacti update" doesn't work after updating sprout graph templates (https://github.com/Metaswitch/chef/issues/211)

*         clearwater-snmp manipulates /etc/snmpd.conf, so snmp doesn't install cleanly (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-infrastructure/issues/186)

*         Clearwater-monit  -- There is no service by that name (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-juju/issues/21)

For upgrading to this release, follow the instructions at http://clearwater.readthedocs.org/en/latest/Upgrading_a_Clearwater_deployment/index.html. If you are deploying an all-in-one node, the standard image (http://vm-images.cw-ngv.com/cw-aio.ova) has been updated for this release.

--
Rob Day
Software Engineer, Project Clearwater

METASWITCH NETWORKS
THE BRAINS OF THE NEW GLOBAL NETWORK
www.metaswitch.com<http://www.metaswitch.com/>

From: Eleanor Merry [mailto:Eleanor.Merry at metaswitch.com]
Sent: Thursday, July 30, 2015 11:34 PM
To: Ratnajit Devnath - ERS, HCL Tech; Clearwater at lists.projectclearwater.org<mailto:Clearwater at lists.projectclearwater.org>
Cc: Ekal Agarwal - ERS, HCL Tech; Ramachandran Sathyanarayanan
Subject: RE: SIP registration failing

Hi,

You need to set the auth. Username in Zoiper to be the private identity of the subscriber - so something like 65055550595@<domain>.

It also looks like there's some issues with Chronos (our timer service - see https://github.com/Metaswitch/chronos/blob/dev/doc/technical.md for more details). Can you please send me your Chronos logs (in /var/log/chronos) and configuration (in /etc/chronos)?

Thanks,
Ellie

Message-ID: <CO1PR02MB24016278BD9B2529C52EDA19B7C0@CO1PR02MB240.namprd02.prod.outlook.com>

Hi Dennis,

It sounds like your shared_config hasn't been shared around the cluster yet, or the underlying etcd cluster hasn't yet formed. Which node do you run upload_shared_config on? Does this report any errors? Can you check whether the etcd cluster is healthy (run 'sudo clearwater-etcdctl cluster health')?

If you're not using our automatic configuration sharing option (detailed here: http://clearwater.readthedocs.org/en/latest/Old_Manual_Install/index.html) then you need to set up the shared_config file before you install the Ellis package.

Ellie

In-Reply-To: <517B603A-78C5-4951-8689-D3CD7822F045@gmail.com>
References: <517B603A-78C5-4951-8689-D3CD7822F045@gmail.com>
Message-ID: <CO1PR02MB2402FB0FC8832BE5D2250BA9B7C0@CO1PR02MB240.namprd02.prod.outlook.com>

Hi Dennis,

It looks from the network trace that Sprout is sending messages to Memento at sip:192.168.1.91;lr. Instead, you should set this to sip:memento at 192.168.1.91:5054;lr;transport=TCP (in your subscribers' IFCs). Please see https://github.com/Metaswitch/memento/blob/dev/docs/memento_overview.md#configuration for more details

Ellie

From: Eleanor Merry [mailto:Eleanor.Merry at metaswitch.com]
Sent: Thursday, July 30, 2015 11:34 PM
To: Ratnajit Devnath - ERS, HCL Tech; Clearwater at lists.projectclearwater.org
Cc: Ekal Agarwal - ERS, HCL Tech; Ramachandran Sathyanarayanan
Subject: RE: SIP registration failing

Hi,

You need to set the auth. Username in Zoiper to be the private identity of the subscriber - so something like 65055550595@<domain>.

It also looks like there's some issues with Chronos (our timer service - see https://github.com/Metaswitch/chronos/blob/dev/doc/technical.md for more details). Can you please send me your Chronos logs (in /var/log/chronos) and configuration (in /etc/chronos)?

Thanks,
Ellie

From Graeme.Robertson at metaswitch.com  Tue Aug 18 13:21:38 2015
From: Graeme.Robertson at metaswitch.com (Graeme Robertson)
Date: Tue, 18 Aug 2015 17:21:38 +0000
Subject: [Clearwater] =?iso-8859-1?q?FW=3A__Louise_de_La_Valli=E8re_releas?=
	=?iso-8859-1?q?e_note?=
In-Reply-To: <DM2PR0201MB0701554FB184AFF3EE98E2F6E3780@DM2PR0201MB0701.namprd02.prod.outlook.com>
References: <DM2PR0201MB0701554FB184AFF3EE98E2F6E3780@DM2PR0201MB0701.namprd02.prod.outlook.com>
Message-ID: <DM2PR0201MB0701CE5CAEB7B22DD7A82E79E3780@DM2PR0201MB0701.namprd02.prod.outlook.com>

Hello,

The release for sprint "Louise de La Valli?re" has been cut.  The code for this release is tagged as release-79 in Github.

We've been working on the following new features in this sprint:

?         We've been continuing to work on our statistics support. Bono and Sprout now expose overload statistics, and we've also been doing some work towards providing stateful statistics in Clearwater in the near future. We're continuing with that in the new sprint.

?         We've added more and improved regressible tests to clearwater-etcd, so that going forward it should be more reliable and more maintainable.

This release includes the following bug fixes:

?         sometimes the features.d directory gets polluted with Debian package files (*.dpkg-*) (https://github.com/Metaswitch/sprout/issues/1174)

?         Monit closes Sprout when registering SNMP tables take too long (https://github.com/Metaswitch/sprout/issues/1150)

?         Assert in pjsip timer when connection fails to SIP peer. (https://github.com/Metaswitch/sprout/issues/1114)

?         Cannot find REGISTER flows in SAS by searching on Call-Id (https://github.com/Metaswitch/sprout/issues/923)

?         No SAS correlation between Clearwater and CFS TAS for 3rd party registrations.  (https://github.com/Metaswitch/sprout/issues/575)

?         Chronos timers overflow giving bad comparisons (TimerStore) (https://github.com/Metaswitch/chronos/issues/156)

?         Makefile doesn't create needed directory (https://github.com/Metaswitch/chronos/issues/153)

?         Chronos performance drop between release-63 and release-72 (https://github.com/Metaswitch/chronos/issues/136)

?         shared_config is not uploaded or applied after a deployment has been spun up (https://github.com/Metaswitch/chef/issues/208)

?         updating a deployment's security groups does not work in a VPC.  (https://github.com/Metaswitch/chef/issues/125)

?         poll_cassandra_ring.sh script doesn't work on multiple networks interfaces (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-cassandra/issues/47)

?         There appears to be a compatibility issue between version  1.2.12 and 2.0.14 when running the spin up new nodes upgrade procedure (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-cassandra/issues/44)

?         clearwater-memcached creates `/etc/init.d/memcached`, which conflicts with memcached (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-infrastructure/issues/121)

?         alarms_agent.cpp is sending traps to the wrong port (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-snmp-handlers/issues/78)

?         alarm_req_listener is not handling zmq_bind error (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-snmp-handlers/issues/77)

?         alarms_agent doesn't log to syslog (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-snmp-handlers/issues/76)

?         clearwater-monit not running after a reboot (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-monit/issues/18)

?         Multiple Networks doc doesn't mention management_local_ip (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-readthedocs/issues/94)

?         Nodes can get stuck in 'finished' state (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-etcd/issues/159)

?         apply_shared_config doesn't bring shared config back into sync when traffic is separated (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-etcd/issues/151)

?         mark_node_failed hangs after completing (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-etcd/issues/150)

?         alarm_constants not included in cluster/config manager eggs (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-etcd/issues/145)

?         The config-manager doesn't correctly update the index when a snapshot invalidates it (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-etcd/issues/139)

?         Simultaneous joins (member add) cause corruption of etcd's datastore (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-etcd/issues/125)

?         When I reboot a group of cluster members (homestead, sprout, ralf), etcd cluster end up "unhealthy" (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-etcd/issues/121)

?         Sometimes when I scale up, the cluster becaomes "unhealthy" (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-etcd/issues/120)

?         Removing dead nodes encounters error, but still works (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-etcd/issues/116)

?         Problem running etcd on system with multiple networks (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-etcd/issues/110)

?         etcd needs manual intervention to recover if the system runs out of space (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-etcd/issues/109)

?         `upload_shared_config` can fail silently (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-etcd/issues/98)

?         Error in script clearwater-auto-config-docker (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-docker/issues/12)

?         When SAS is taken down while running traffic, excessive error logs are generated (https://github.com/Metaswitch/sas-client/issues/46)

?         SNMP stats occasionally come back wrong, failing the tests (https://github.com/Metaswitch/clearwater-fv-test/issues/22)

For upgrading to this release, follow the instructions at http://clearwater.readthedocs.org/en/latest/Upgrading_a_Clearwater_deployment/index.html. If you are deploying an all-in-one node, the standard image (http://vm-images.cw-ngv.com/cw-aio.ova) has been updated for this release.

Thanks,
Graeme

Hi Claudio,

Our SIPp stress scripts assume that the users have a password of 7kkzTyGW ? this is hardcoded at https://github.com/Metaswitch/sprout/blob/master/clearwater-sip-stress.root/usr/share/clearwater/infrastructure/scripts/sip-stress#L13.

Our bulk provisioning instructions (https://github.com/Metaswitch/crest/blob/dev/docs/Bulk-Provisioning%20Numbers.md) include instructions for bulk-provisioning users with this password (see the section starting ?If you are provisioning numbers for SIPp stress testing, you will need to force them all to use the password '7kkzTyGW'. This CSV file can be generated with??). Our bulk provisioning scripts handle the conversion of that password into the SIP Digest HA1 (the MD5 hashing process you refer to).

Note that this requires command-line bulk provisioning ? there?s no way to force a password of 7kkzTyGW through the Ellis UI.

Does that give you what you need to know? Please let me know if you have any other questions.

Best,
Rob

Rob Day
Software Engineer, Project Clearwater

From Eleanor.Merry at metaswitch.com  Tue Aug 25 12:54:30 2015
From: Eleanor.Merry at metaswitch.com (Eleanor Merry)

In-Reply-To: <1194055668.8915501.1440263130374.JavaMail.yahoo@mail.yahoo.com>
References: <1194055668.8915501.1440263130374.JavaMail.yahoo@mail.yahoo.com>
Message-ID: <CO1PR02MB2403A6B1DC8DF3C03AB96FC9B610@CO1PR02MB240.namprd02.prod.outlook.com>

Hi Tam,

It looks like the ACK is being rejected because the Session Expires value is too high. This is because the max_session_expires value wasn?t being correctly passed into Sprout. I?ve raised an issue for this (you can see this at https://github.com/Metaswitch/sprout/issues/1180), and I?ve put a fix into Sprout.

If you urgently need this fix, you can pull it from the ?latest? repo, although please note that it hasn?t gone through our full end of release QA. Our next stable release that contains this fix will be released in the next week.

If you want to use the fix in the ?latest? repo, then you should edit /etc/apt/sources.list.d/clearwater.list/ so that it contains ?deb http://repo.cw-ngv.com/latest binary/?, and then run ?sudo clearwater-upgrade? on all of your Clearwater nodes to install the new version.

Ellie

From Eleanor.Merry at metaswitch.com  Fri Aug 28 11:05:05 2015
From: Eleanor.Merry at metaswitch.com (Eleanor Merry)
Date: Fri, 28 Aug 2015 15:05:05 +0000
Subject: [Clearwater] change domain in the All-in-One OVF installation
In-Reply-To: <CP1PR80MB128684DD895DD0EF7B404358A96F0@CP1PR80MB1286.lamprd80.prod.outlook.com>
References: <CP1PR80MB128684DD895DD0EF7B404358A96F0@CP1PR80MB1286.lamprd80.prod.outlook.com>
Message-ID: <CO1PR02MB240A5E3B61A120593939CF89B6E0@CO1PR02MB240.namprd02.prod.outlook.com>

Hi Felipe,

You can, but this will make any subscribers you've already created invalid.

To change the configuration, change home_domain in /etc/clearwater/shared_config to your desired value, and then run 'sudo service clearwater-infrastructure restart' and 'sudo monit restart all'.

You'll  also need to re-run the create_numbers script (https://github.com/Metaswitch/ellis/blob/dev/docs/create-numbers.md) on Ellis to populate its numbers pool with subscribers with the new home domain.

Ellie
